    15→    const { name, description, agentIds, type, chiefOfStaffId } = body  
    16→  
    17→    if (!name || typeof name !== 'string') {

    20→

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { loadGovernance, setPassword, verifyPassword } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→  
     4→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     5→  try {  
     6→    const body = await request.json()  
     7→    const { password, currentPassword } = body  
     8→  
     9→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string' || password.length < 6) {  
    10→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }, { status: 400 })  
    11→    }  
    12→  
    13→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    14→  
    15→    // If password already set, require current password  
    16→    if (config.passwordHash) {  
    17→      if (!currentPassword || !verifyPassword(currentPassword)) {  
    18→        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid current password' }, { status: 401 })  
    19→      }  
    20→    }  
    21→  
    22→    setPassword(password)  
    23→    return NextResponse.json({ success: true })  
    24→  } catch (error) {  
    25→    console.error('Failed to set password:', error)  
    26→    return NextResponse.json(  
    27→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to set password' },  
    28→      { status: 500 }  
    29→    )  
    30→  }  
    31→}

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { verifyPassword, setManager, removeManager, loadGovernance } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→import { getAgent } from '@/lib/agent-registry'  
     4→  
     5→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     6→  try {  
     7→    const body = await request.json()  
     8→    const { agentId, password } = body  
     9→  
    10→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string') {  
    11→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    12→    }  
    13→  
    14→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    15→    if (!config.passwordHash) {  
    16→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password not set. Set a password first via POST /api/governance/password' }, { status: 400 })  
    17→    }  
    18→  
    19→    if (!verifyPassword(password)) {  
    20→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid governance password' }, { status: 401 })  
    21→    }  
    22→  
    23→    if (agentId === null) {  
    24→      removeManager()  
    25→      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, managerId: null })  
    26→    }  
    27→  
    28→    if (typeof agentId !== 'string' || !agentId.trim()) {  
    29→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId must be a non-empty string or null' }, { status: 400 })  
    30→    }  
    31→  
    32→    // Verify agent exists  
    33→    const agent = getAgent(agentId)  
    34→    if (!agent) {  
    35→      return NextResponse.json({ error: `Agent '${agentId}' not found` }, { status: 404 })  
    36→    }  
    37→  
    38→    setManager(agentId)  
    39→    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, managerId: agentId, managerName: agent.name || agent.alias })  
    40→  } catch (error) {  
    41→    console.error('Failed to set manager:', error)  
    42→    return NextResponse.json(  
    43→      { error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Failed to set manager' },  
    44→      { status: 500 }  
    45→    )  
    46→  }  
    47→}

     1→/**  
     2→ * Transfer Requests API  
     3→ * GET - List transfer requests (optionally filtered by teamId or agentId)

    10→import { isManager, isChiefOfStaffAnywhere } from '@/lib/governance'  
    11→  
    12→export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {  
    13→  try {  
    14→    const teamId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('teamId')  
    15→    const agentId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('agentId')  
    16→    const status = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('status') // 'pending', 'approved', 'rejected', or null for all  
    17→  
    18→    let requests = loadTransfers()  
    19→  
    20→    if (teamId) {  
    21→      requests = requests.filter(r => r.fromTeamId === teamId || r.toTeamId === teamId)  
    22→    }  
    23→    if (agentId) {  
    24→      requests = requests.filter(r => r.agentId === agentId)  
    25→    }  
    26→    if (status) {  
    27→      requests = requests.filter(r => r.status === status)  
    28→    }  
    29→  
    30→    return NextResponse.json({ requests })  
    31→  } catch (error) {  
    32→    console.error('Error loading transfers:', error)  
    33→    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Internal server error' }, { status: 500 })  
    34→  }  
    35→}

<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `route.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

**File:** `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/api/governance/transfers/[id]/resolve/route.ts`  

**Old:**  
```
      const fromTeamAgentIds = fromTeam.agentIds.filter(aid => aid !== transferReq.agentId)
      updateTeam(fromTeam.id, { agentIds: fromTeamAgentIds })

      // Add agent to destination team

        const toTeamAgentIds = [...toTeam.agentIds, transferReq.agentId]
        updateTeam(toTeam.id, { agentIds: toTeamAgentIds })
```

**New:**  
```
      const fromTeamAgentIds = fromTeam.agentIds.filter(aid => aid !== transferReq.agentId)
      await updateTeam(fromTeam.id, { agentIds: fromTeamAgentIds })

      // Add agent to destination team
      if (toTeam && !toTeam.agentIds.includes(transferReq.agentId)) {
        const toTeamAgentIds = [...toTeam.agentIds, transferReq.agentId]
        await updateTeam(toTeam.id, { agentIds: toTeamAgentIds })
```

**Result:**

**Agent:** `spark` | **Description:** Fix team-registry test awaits  

Fix the test file `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/tests/team-registry.test.ts`.  

The functions `createTeam`, `updateTeam`, and `deleteTeam` from `@/lib/team-registry` are now async (they return Promises). The test file calls them without `await`, causing all tests that use these functions to fail.  

You need to:  
1. Read the file  
2. Add `await` before every call to `createTeam(`, `updateTeam(`, and `deleteTeam(` in the test functions  
3. Make any test callback function that uses `await` into an `async` function (change `() =>` to `async () =>` or `it('name', () =>` to `it('name', async () =>`)  
4. Also add a mock for `@/lib/file-lock` (the file-lock module is now imported by team-registry): Add this mock BEFORE the imports of the module under test:  
```typescript
vi.mock('@/lib/file-lock', () => ({
  withLock: vi.fn((_name: string, fn: () => any) => Promise.resolve(fn())),
}))
```
5. Run `yarn test tests/team-registry.test.ts` to verify all tests pass  

REPORTING RULES:  
- Return to orches

| 9 | No loading state on transfer buttons | Added `resolvingTransferId` state + disabled (commit `ca465a8`) |

## <span style="color:#FFC107">◇ ASSISTANT</span>  *[2026-02-16 17:28:04]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #FFC107; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Dev server is running on `http://localhost:23000` with the `feature/team-governance` branch.  

**What to test:**  

1. **Role assignment** — Open any agent profile, click "+ Assign Role", select MANAGER. You'll be prompted to set the governance password (first time). After setting it, the MANAGER badge should appear.  

2. **COS assignment** — Open another agent's profile, assign Chief-of-Staff, select a closed team. Enter the governance password.  

3. **Demote** — Click the role badge on a role-assigned agent, select Normal Agent, enter password.  

4. **Team membership** — In the agent profile, use the Teams section to join/leave teams. Normal agents can only join open teams; MANAGER/COS can join any.  

5. **Transfer flow** — If an agent is in a closed team, joining another team creates a transfer request needing COS approval. The approve/reject buttons appear for the source team's COS.  

6. **Messaging filter** — In MessageCenter compose, autocomplete should only show reachable agents based on governance rules.  

When you're done testing, let me know and I'll stop the dev server and restart PM2.  

</div>

**Old:**  
```
describe('createTeam', () => {
  it('creates a team with name and agentIds', () => {
    const team = createTeam({ name: 'New Team', agentIds: ['a1'] })

    expect(team.name).toBe('New Team')
    expect(team.agentIds).toEqual(['a1'])
    expect(team.id).toMatch(/^uuid-/)
  })

  it('creates a team with empty agentIds', () => {
    const team = createTeam({ name: 'Empty', agentIds: [] })

    expect(team.agentIds).toEqual([])
  })

  it('sets optional description', () => {
    const team = createTeam({ name: 'Described', description: 'A description', agentIds: [] })
    expect(team.description).toBe('A description')
  })

  it('persists to storage', () => {
    createTeam({ name: 'Persisted', agentIds: [] })

    const teams = loadTeams()
    expect(teams).toHaveLength(1)
    expect(teams[0].name).toBe('Persisted')
  })
})
```

**New:**  
```
describe('createTeam', () => {
  it('creates a team with name and agentIds', async () => {
    const team = await createTeam({ name: 'New Team', agentIds: ['a1'] })

    expect(team.name).toBe('New Team')
    expect(team.agentIds).toEqual(['a1'])
    expect(team.id).toMatch(/^uuid-/)
  })

  it('creates a team with empty agentIds', async () => {
    const team = await createTeam({ name: 'Empty', agentIds: [] })

    expect(team.agentIds).toEqual([])
  })

  it('sets optional description', async () => {
    const team = await createTeam({ name: 'Described', description: 'A description', agentIds: [] })
    expect(team.description).toBe('A description')
  })

  it('persists to storage', async () => {
    await createTeam({ name: 'Persisted', agentIds: [] })

    const teams = loadTeams()
    expect(teams).toHaveLength(1)
    expect(teams[0].name).toBe('Persisted')
  })
})
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/tests/team-registry.test.ts has been updated successfully.

  })

  it('returns false for non-existent team', () => {
    expect(deleteTeam('non-existent')).toBe(false)
  })

  it('preserves other teams', () => {
    const team1 = createTeam({ name: 'Keep', agentIds: [] })
    const team2 = createTeam({ name: 'Delete', agentIds: [] })

    deleteTeam(team2.id)

    const remaining = loadTeams()
    expect(remaining).toHaveLength(1)
    expect(remaining[0].id).toBe(team1.id)
  })
})
```

**New:**  
```
describe('deleteTeam', () => {
  it('deletes team and returns true', async () => {
    const team = await createTeam({ name: 'Delete Me', agentIds: [] })
    const result = await deleteTeam(team.id)

    expect(result).toBe(true)
    expect(loadTeams()).toHaveLength(0)
  })

  it('returns false for non-existent team', async () => {
    expect(await deleteTeam('non-existent')).toBe(false)
  })

  it('preserves other teams', async () => {
    const team1 = await createTeam({ name: 'Keep', agentIds: [] })
    const team2 = await createTeam({ name: 'Delete', agentIds: [] })

    await deleteTeam(team2.id)

    const remaining = loadTeams()
    expect(remaining).toHaveLength(1)
    expect(remaining[0].id).toBe(team1.id)
  })
})
```
